<br> Taki was a small, peculiar creature. He carried a cane and a top hat. [[Top hat?->tophat]] [[Cane?->cane]]The top hat almost eclipsed his head and covered his eyes. <br> <br> [[Next->meetingtako]]His cane was rather small and twice the length of his arms. <br> <br> [[Next->meetingtako]]Taki is standing in a forest. on a well-worn path. The trees and bushes tower over Taki and he feels intimidated. [[Continue on the path->almost-shrine]] [[Turn around and go back->backwards]]Taki walks up the path, past a small stream and into a small clearing.<br><br> [[Next->tako]]Taki turns around and walks back down the path, into a small clearing.<br><br> [[Next->tako]]The clearing has a hut in it, with a wisp of smoke trickling out the chimney. The window is lit up with light from the fire and it flickers occasionally.<br><br> [[Enter hut->takoshut]] [[Explore past the clearing->shrine]]The hut has little furniture -- only a fireplace, table, and one chair. The table is scattered with journals in indecipherable handwriting and half-empty cups of tea, and it seems that most of them are about a week old.<br><br> [[Back outside->clearing]]Taki takes the trail, which curves around the hut and into the forest. The trail takes him over a large gulley and into an even smaller clearing in an older section of the forest, in which Taki cannot see the top of the shortest trees.<br><br> [[Next->takoshiding]]The clearing has a hut in it, with a wisp of smoke oozing out the stovepipe. The window radiates with firelight and flickers every so often.<br><br> [[Explore past the clearing->shrine]]Taki continues on the path for a short distance to the other side of the clearing, where he finds a large stone with some engravings on it. The rock seems to be a shrine, and there's a lump of cloth on the far side of the rock.<br><br> [[Investigate the cloth->shrine-farside]] [[Continue on the path->river]]Taki walks to the other side of the rock and finds a burlap sack, round in shape, lying on the ground.<br> [[Open sack->freetako]]The path leads Taki to a large, rushing river. After a moment of panic, Taki realizes there's a bridge a couple hundred feet up the river. <br> "Hello, I'm Tako," says Tako. <br> <br> [[Next->almost-end]]"I'm running from some incorporeal feeling," says the smaller creature, who introduces himself as Tako.<br> While Taki takes a moment to try to figure this out, Tako yells again and runs behind a tree. Taki realizes, just a moment too late, that he was standing with one foot on the bridge, and one foot on the bank of the river, and the bridge was about to collapse from an unseen weight.<br> Taki jumps back just in time as the bridge collapses and falls with a <i>splash</i> into the rushing river.<br> [[Next->end]]Taki introduces himself and they have a small chat. <br><br> Taki decides not to ask why Tako was hiding in a burlap sack next to a large rock. [[Next->end]]Tako leads Taki back to the hut in the clearing, which turns out to be Tako's house, and invites him in for a cup of tea. Taki accepts and Taki and Tako spend a pleasant afternoon together.
